There is a way in which you should make three or four cauteries, lining them along the length of the mouse, according to the shape of the liver cauterizer that we have mentioned before; and do not press your hand on the entire cauterizer, and let the hairs be near its back; and another way of cauterizing is that you heat the cauterizer that has two needles, as we have shown in the dislocation of the shoulder; and relieve the pain where it comes from the left side, and let the elevations that you relieve the pain along the curve, according to the length of the body, and the cauterizer should be according to the width of the body.
Aprés i boute les II ners enflamez tant que li keurs soit perciez de l’autre part, et puis trai fuers le cautere, et ensi en i avra IIII Et se tu vues, si cauterize a tot le cautere a III ners.	After boiling the two needles until the one on the other side is perceived to be hot, then remove the cauterizer, and thus in it will have four. And if you see, if it is cauterized with the entire cauterizer at three needles.
Aprés le cure quant il a geteit porriture par lonc tens, et ce vaut mues que li autre des cures devant dites.	After healing when it has gotten pus due to long tension, and this is worth mentioning as another cure before mentioned.
de ydropisie	of hydropsy
Cautere ne vaut a ydropique, fors c’a la maniere qui est apelee «asclytes».	Cauterization is not useful for hydropsy, except in the manner which is called "ascites".
Quant tu la cures selonc les manieres que nos avons dit en divisions, et ta cure ne profite mie, adonques covient il que tu li faices IIII cauteres entor la boude, et I sus l’estomac, et un sus le foie, et I sus la mice, et II derrier le dos sus l’espinee, et I endroit le pis; et soit li cauteres bien pres de l’espés dou keur.	When you treat it according to the methods that we have mentioned in divisions, and your treatment does not work, then it is necessary that you make four cauterizations around the belly, and one above the stomach, and one above the liver, and one in the groin, and one behind the back on the spine, and one at the worst place; and let the cauterizations be very close to the skin.
Aprés laisse le cautere aovert por giter porriture lonc tens, et ne lassier mie la cure dou malaide aprés le cautere; et sanation se hasterait, et seront ensamble les II ententions avec l’aide de Deu.	After the fire cauterization for the purpose of healing, do not neglect the care of the wound after the cauterization; and healing will hasten, and together with the help of God, both intentions will be achieved.
Li forme dou cautere por le ventre soit li clavile que nos avons devant mostreit; et cil por le dos soit olivaire, selonc ceu qu’il est ci devant mis.	The shape of the fire cauterization for the abdomen is a clamp that we have shown before; and for the back, it is an oil lamp, as it has been placed before.
de l’enfleure des piez	of the swelling of the feet
Quant li piez sont enflez a celui qui est ydropique, et sont plain d’awe citrine, il covient que tu cauterizes sus le dos dou piet entre l’auriculaire et l’anulaire; et lieve ta main avec le cautere sens torner.	When the feet are swollen and have plain yellow spots, it is necessary to cauterize above the foot between the auricular and annular; and release your hand with the cauterization towards returning.
Et n’entrer mie trop em parfont, ensi sarrait fuers li awe citrine, et soit li cauteres selonc cest forme:	And do not enter too deeply into the flesh, thus avoiding the danger of the knife, and let the cauteries be done in this manner:
Aprés fai sus II jambes II cauteres en chescune jambe a la pointe dou cutellaire; et soit li cauteres dou lonc, l’un desoz le genoil devant et l’autre defuers, enmi la jambe; et laisse les cauteres aovers longement sens curer, que li awe en isse; aprés le cure des autres cures que nos avons dit.	After making incisions above the two knees, apply two cauteries in each leg at the tip of the short knife; and let the cauteries be long, one on the front of the knee and the other on the back, inside the leg; and leave the cauteries hanging for a long time to cure the wound that has been made.
de la menoison	of the bandage
Quant solution de ventre vient de froidor et de moistor, tant que li vertus retentive et digestive qui est ou stomac et en l’intestine est afleboie, et ne puet estre curez par manieres de cures; et tu vois le malaide bien soffrant et de fort vertut, si fai I grant cautere sus l’estomac selonc ceu qu’il en a parleit ci devant ou cautere de l’estomac, au cautere circule; et IIII cauteres entor la boude subtilz a tout I cautere clavile subtil, et II cauteres sus les hainches.	When the belly is cold and wet, as long as the retentive and digestive virtues which are in the stomach and intestines are blocked, and cannot be cured by other methods; and you see the patient suffering greatly and with great pain, then make a large cauterization above the stomach according to what has been said before about cauterizing the stomach, and circulate the cauterization; and four cauterizations around the belly, tightly tied, and two cauterizations on the hips.
Et se tu vois les moistors habundans et le malaide soffrant, se li fai cautere sus le poignil, et I cautere sus chaicun yle, et II petis cauteres sus l’estomac delez le grant, car li cure est profitans quant il i a bone aide.	If you see the moisture abundant and the pain suffering, then make fire cauterization above the knuckle, and I cauterization above each rib, and II small cauterizations above the stomach below the great one, for the cure is beneficial when it has good help.
de la cure des emorroydes	of the treatment of worms
Quant les emorroydes sont ou fondement, ou une ou plusors, et sont ancienes et sont de grosses humors froides et moistes corrumpues, et sont curees si com nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne profite mie, si fai cauteres: III sus l’espine dou dos, celi qui est tout defuers desoz almecdate poc et poc en triangulant, et I cautere desoz la boude II dois; et se tu penses que ses estomac soit refroidiez, et li viande ne cuise, et on voit enfler la faice, adonques li faice on I grant cautere sus le stomac, si com il est devant dit, et I autre sus le foie, et I autre sus la mice a tout le cautere clavile; et laisse le cautere overt lonc tens. de la charnositeit qui est nommee «thelul»	of the cartilage that is called "thelul

When you cut through the cartilage, if the cauterizing iron seems like a razor, and then put it all on fire over the cartilage cut; and leave your hand so that the cauterizer comes to the base of the vein, from which the blood flows; do this once or twice, and if there is much cartilage, cauterize each part as we have said; after curing the wounds until they are healed; and if you cauterize with a large cauterizing iron above the cartilage, it will have greater help.
de plaie mal curee	of poorly treated wound
Quant li malaides ne puet soffrir tailleure ne overture, que nos raconterons en son leu, si vient teil maladie que ne puet estre sanee fuer que par cautere.	When the wounds cannot bear the incision or opening, we will tell you about it in its place, so that an illness comes that cannot be healed except by cauterization.
Quant a aucun vient fistule, et est enveillie et giete porriture et moistors corrumpues, si la doies prover a tot une tente subtil, et garde que tu saiches a tot la tente combien elle a de parfont.	When any fistula comes and is awakened and poured with pus and corrupted moisture, then you should prove to all a thin tent, and guard that you clean the tent as much as it has of porosity.
Aprés eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et le boute en la fistule selonc la quantiteit que li tente i est entrée, et rencomence lou cautere tant que cil cors porris et corrumpus soient ars, une fois, ou II ou III, selonc la quantiteit de som besoing; et te warde d’ardre lé nerf qui sunt enqui, et des grans voinnes.	After the cauterizing iron is heated to the point where it seems like a razor, and the cautery is inserted into the fistula according to the quantity that the tent has entered, and you start again with the cauterization until those who are in there and corrupted are burned, once, or two, or three, depending on the amount of pain; and be careful not to burn the nerves which are inside, and the large veins.
se li fistule vait au cors de la vesie et a l’intestine, si te warde de ces leus, et ne faire ceu fuers que en leu charnut, et pense qu’ele n’est mie persans; aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez, et se li leus est saielez, et les matieres sont ostees lonc tens, adonc saiches que li leus est sanez entierement; et se les matieres ne sont ostees, saiche que li leus est troez, et corrumpus li os au font; et ensi com un de ces que nos dirons en son leu.	If the fistula goes to the center of the bladder and intestine, you should avoid these things, and only do this in the case where it is necessary, and think that it is not yet cured; after curing the limb as long as it is healthy, and if the limbs are sewn, and the matters are removed slowly, then wash the limbs completely; and if the matters are not removed, sew the limbs and corrupt the bone at the font; and thus, like one of those that we will say in its limb.
de la maladie des reins	of the disease of the kidneys

de la vessie	of the bladder

de la marris	of the marsh

de la hainche	of the waist

When viscous moisture descends to the waist bone, and for this reason it moves out of its place, and the signs are that the thigh is longer than the other when measured together; and the muscles of the buttocks are found to be separated, it is necessary that you cauterize the pain above the waist bone with a cautery similar to a circle, and sign before the belly around the waist as it turns, so that the waist is inside the circle; and if it is such a cauterization as has been done on the stomach.

de la dolor de la hainche	of the pain of the hip

When pain comes in the hip joint, and it is from cold and moisture, and the evils are caused by what we have said in the division and the cure does not work, and the disease is ancient: then it is necessary that you purge the evil of large humors with fetid pills, or other good-quality pills similar.
Aprés li fai cautere; et li maniere dou cautere si est selonc II manieres: c’est a savoir ensamble medicines ardans, et cautere de feu.	After the fomentation; and the manner of the cauterization is as follows: it is to say together with burning medicines, and fire cauterization.

Et se tu vues, si le cauterize au cautere dou cercle que nos avons devant dit en la dislocation de la hainche; mais fai en teil maniere que li cercles conteigne toute la hainche, et tous li espés dou keur soit ars.	And if you see, the cauterization with the cautery in the form of a circle that we have previously mentioned in the dislocation of the shoulder; but do it in a different way so that the circle contains the whole shoulder, and all the tendons are burned.

Et se mestiers est, se li en fai plus; et se il seit que li dolor soit desoz le genoil vers la cuisse, se li fais cautere au cautere cutellaire ou circulaire, et te done bien garde en tous tes cauteres que tu n’i lassier mie tant le cautere que tu brules les ners et les grans arteres, et que tu ne faices au malaide plus grant nuisance et contraction.	And if the profession is, do it more; and if the pain is dislocated from the groin towards the thigh, do cauterization with the cauterizing knife or circular, and be careful in all your cauterizations that you do not tire yourself too much with the cautery that you burn the nerves and the large arteries, and that you do not cause greater harm and contraction.
Et je meisme ai veus plusors qui ont fait cautere sus la cheville dou piet, et li lasserent tant que li jambe fut toute enflee, et li piez ausi, et fut perciez et corrumpus toz li piez.	And I have seen many who have cauterized above the ankle, and they tired themselves so much that the leg was completely numb, and the foot also, and all the feet were rotten and corrupted.

Et se li dolors est en II parties ensamble, fai cautere en l’une et en l’autre, selonc ceste maniere.	And if the pain is on both sides together, perform cauterization on one and the other, in this manner.

Albucasim says that we use little of this cauterizing iron because of the fear of its appearance, and it is not seen by many who use it; however, this is a good cauterizing iron, which can bear the pain, and where it is applied.

de la dolor dou dos	of the pain of two arms

de la dolor des jointes	of the pain of the joints
Quant dolor de jointes sunt de moistors que sont espandues a chaicun membre dou cors, et quant dolor vient em piez, que li mire apelent «podagre» proprement, et quant elle est de froide cause et cures de medicines ne la puent curer, si est curez par cauteres en teil maniere: fai li mout de cauteres entor la jointure dou piet, et soit li cauteres olivaire selonc ceste forme:	When the pain of the joints is due to moisture that has spread to each limb of the body, and when the pain comes from the feet, which is properly called "podagra", and when it is caused by cold and cannot be cured by medicines, then it must be treated with cauterization in this manner: apply a large amount of cauterization around the joint, and let the cauterizing oil be applied in this form:
Et s’il i a besoigne que tu poignes sus la faice dou piet, se li fai cautere a tot le cautere c’on claime «point».	And if there is a need to hold the face down with the knife, then perform the entire cauterization with the "point" that is claimed.
Et se les dolors viegnent jusc’a genous et as autres jointures, et ceu avient maintes fois, se li fai cautere sus chaicun genoil III cauteres ou IIII de chescunne partie, a tout le cautere olivaire; et se tu as mestier de plus, si en fai plus, mais n’i tenir mie ta main fuers que tant que li espés dou keur soit ars.	And if the pains come from the joint and other joints, and it happens often, then perform cauterization on each joint with three or four cautery irons of each part, at every cauterization; and if you have more skill, do so, but do not hold your hand farther than the end of the handle of the knife.
Et se les dolors dessendent jusc’a genoil et au dos, se li aministre le cautere que nos avons dit en son chapistre.	And if the pains descend to the joint and the back, then administer the cauterization that we have said in its chapter.
Et se les dolors sunt as mains, si fai poins entor le foscile II lignes; et s’il remaint point de dolor as dois, si fai poins sus chescune jointe et sus lou poil de la main; et se les dolors vienent jusc’as coutes ou jusc’as espaules, si cauterize chescune partie, et fai boin governement au malaide et penre medicines.	And if the pains are on the fingers, make points around the nail two lines; and if they do not remain in place, make points above each joint and above the hair of the hand; and if the pains come from the wrist or shoulder, cauterize each part, and provide good management and proper medicines.
Car se tu li fais boin governement et tu purges fleume, si sera saneis a l’aide de Deu.	For if you provide good management and purge the humor, it will be healed with the help of God.
de la routure dou syfac	of the wound from the tooth
Quant routure vient en angres, et li bouelz dessendent as coions et c’est novelement, si covient que quant tu lou vues curer, qu’il ne menjuce mie celui jor; et qu’il use choses qui laichent lou ventre, si que li fiens dessende de son ventre; aprés le fai seoir sus son dos entre tes mains, et li comande qu’il teigne son alaine tant que li boueil soient repairiet, et les ramoinne a tes dois, et seigne d’enche desoz la routure sus l’os dou poignil, et a tout un signe que soit semblans a la moitiet d’un cercle a desus dou cors; puis eschaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	When a wound comes from an angle, and the pus descends to the groin and it is newly formed, then when you see it to be healed, that it does not move much that day; and that you use things that relieve the stomach, so that the pain decreases from his belly; afterwards make him sit on his back between your hands, and command him to keep his arm straight until the pus is repairiet, and the pain is gone, and signify a sign that is like half of a circle above the wound over the bone of the wrist, then warm the cauterizing iron:
tant qu’il soit blans et qu’il giete senteles.	until it is white and drips honey.
Puis ramoine les bouels a lor leu; et li ministres teigne sa main sus qu’il ne retornent arrier; et oevre bien les cuisses au malaide, et met desoz lui I cussin et I serjant sus les cuisses, et I autre sus lou pis qui li teigne les mains; puis met le cautere sus lou signe a tout ta main, et lou tien droit et lou tien tant que tu ateignes l’os, et se tu ne l’ateins la premiere fois, si le rencomence encor une autre tant que tu viegnes jusc’a l’os; et te warde subtilment que li boueil ne saille quant tu fais lou cautere; que tu ne le brulasses; et que par ceu li malaides ne muere, ou autre malz.	Then remove the dirt from the joint; and the minister stains his hand above so that it does not return backwards; and work well on the thighs at the shoulder, and put disinfectant and serum on the thighs, and the other on the lowest part that stains the hands; then put the cautery on the sign all over your hand, and hold the right and left until you reach the bone, and if you do not reach it the first time, start again with another until you come close to the bone; and be careful that the dirt does not come out when you do the cautery; that you do not burn it; and that by this the pain does not die, or other harm.
Et saiches que quant tu ne viens jusc’a l’os au cautere, tes ovraiges ne vaut rien.	And if you do not apply the fire cautery to the bone, your work is worthless.
Et covient que li cauteres des enfans soit subtilz selonc la mesure d’ous, et des grans gens aussi grans selonc lor mesure; aprés III jors cure lou leu dou cautere de burre tant que li eschaudure soit ostee; aprés le cure d’autres oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez, et gise li malaides XL jors sus son dos tant que li plaie soit bien soudee; et covient que ses norrissemens soit lassatis longement, si que li boueil ne saillent quant il se preigdra d’aler en chambres.	And it is necessary that the cauterizer for children be subtle according to their age, and for adults as large as they are; after three days care for the wound of the fire cautery until the eschar is formed; then care for other wounds until they are healed, and grind the hairs on their back for forty days until the wound is well scarred; and it is necessary that their movements be restricted for a long time, so that the blisters do not form when they move.
Et aprés XL jors, quant il se voudra lever, se li amenistre une faixe bien faite, et la porse XL autres jors; et ait boin repos, qu’il se travaille poc et se warde de trop grant repletion de boivre et de mengier, et de trop haut braire; et quant il fait cest enseignement si est sanez entierement.	After forty days, when he wishes to get up, let him be fed a well-cooked meal, and for the next forty days; and let him have good rest, that he works little and avoids too much repletion from drinking and eating, and too much heat; and when he follows this instruction, he is completely healed.
Et je dirai ci aprés la cure de taillier en son chapistre.	I will tell you about the treatment after cutting into his chapter.
de la routure dou ventre	of the rupture of the belly
Quant routures vienent en autres ventres et sont connisans, et tu vues qu’elles ne croissent plus, se li fai I cautere dou cautere reont selonc sa quantiteit, et soit ars li tiers dou keur; aprés le cure selonc ceu que nos avons dit; et aucun des anciens ont dit c’on le doit cauterizer au cautere a III angles selonc ceste forme:	When ruptures come in other bellies and are known, and you see that they do not grow anymore, let him have the fire cautery according to its quantity, and let it be applied to one third of the wound; after the treatment as we have said; and no ancient ones have said that it should be cauterized with the cautery at three angles in this form:
mais signe premier le leu d’enche et fai une ligne per la largesce desus la routure, et une autre defuers, et main ta main emmi a tout le cautere clavile.	but the first sign is the shoulder blade protruding and make a line across the width of the rip, and another below, and hold your hand to all the burning cautery.
Mais li premiers cauteres est plus legiers et muedres.	But the first burns are lighter and more painless.
de dolor anciene en aucun membre	of ancient pain in any limb
Quant dolor vient en aucun membre, ou de cheoir ou de ferir, et cele dolor tient lonc tens, et li cure de medicine n’i vaut, adonc covient qu’il soit cauterizeis au cautere qui est apelez «poins», et soit li cauteres selonc la longesce dou membre et la petitece et sa foibleteit et sa vertut et sa location de torcions et de sa dolor.	When pain comes in any limb, whether it is to fall or to strike, and this pain lasts long, and the medical cure does not help, then it must be cauterized with the burning iron called "pons", and the cauteries should be according to the length of the limb and its smallness and weakness and its strength and its location of twists and its pain.
s’il est sanez dou premier cautere, c’est bien; se ceu nom, recomence I autre cautere sus celui, car teilz costume est qu’il se doit muer au membre que li est prochiens, por coi il covient que tu faices les cauteres tant que li malaides soit saneis.	If the first cautery is healthy and well-done, it's good; if not, start another cautery above the first one, as it is customary that it should be applied to the member that is nearest, because you must do the cauterizations until the hairs are healed.
de meselerie	to cauterize
Li meseil sont aidiet aucune fois par cautere par grant aide, et meismement li maladie que vient de la putrefaction de fleume et de melancolie.	Cauterization is never done without great help, and at the same time the disease that comes from the putrefaction of pus and melancholy.
Cant tu la vues cauterizer, pren warde se li maladie est au comencement, et s’ele est curee selonc ceu que nos avons dit en la division, et ne dessent ne ne demoure, et tu doutes que li corruption ne porpreigne tout le malaide, adonques li fai V cauteres sus lou chief: I emmi le chief a nouf, et l’autre vers lou front a la fin des chevous; et II sus les II cornes, et I derrierre sus le haiterel; et i laise tant ta main que li cauteres viegne jusc’a l’os, et tant que les escorces en issent fors si que les vapors des grosses humors s’en puissent issir; et le cauterize sus la mice selonc ce qu’il est devant.	If you see that the cauterization is done, take precaution if the disease is at the beginning, and if it has been cured according to what we have said in the division, and does not spread or remain, and you doubt that the corruption will not spread throughout the wound, then do three cauterizations above the head: I bring the head to the nose, and the other towards the forehead at the end of the cheeks; and II above the two corners, and I behind the neck; and leave as much hand as the cauterization reaches the bone, and as long as the scabs come out so that the vapors of the large humors can escape; and cauterize the wound according to what is in front.
Et se li meselerie est partout esparse; et elle pert manifestement, si covient que tu lou cauterizes de ces cauteres que nos avons dit ou chief, et I cautere en som lou neis, et II cauteres sus l’espinee dou col, et VI cauteres sus l’espinee dou dos, et I grant sus la crupie et I autre delez, et II sus les II espaules; et II sus les coutes, et II sus les tendrons dou pis, et I sus chascune jointe des mains et des piez, et sus les fosses des mains; et te warde des ners que sunt sus lou derrien calcant, que tu ne les bruler; et aucune fois fait om cautere sus l’os dou poignil, et I autre sus l’os de l’estomac, et I autre sus lou foie.	And if the injury is widely spread; and it is clearly apparent, so you should cauterize with these cauteries that we have said or chief, and the cautery in the nose, and two cauteries above the spine of the neck, and six cauteries above the spine of the back, and one great one above the buttocks and one other below, and two above the shoulders, and two above the elbows, and two above the knees, and one above each joint of the hands and feet, and above the wounds of the hands; and beware of those that are above the lower back calcifying, that you do not burn them; and never make a cautery above the bone of the little finger, and one above the bone of the stomach, and one above the liver.
Et saiches que quant plus i fais de cautere, plus li fais d’aide, et mues li profite; et saiches que li malaides ne sent point de dolor au cautere si com li sain le sentent, por ce que li cors est ja toz corrumpus.	And the more you do cauterization, the less you need to help, and it benefits him; and know that the pain is not felt as much in cauterization as it is felt by the healthy one, because the body is already corrupted.
Et covient ke li cautere soient grant et petit selonc les membres et les jointures, selonc ceu que vos lou troverez en manieres des fers.	It should be large and small according to the limbs and joints, according to what you will find in the manner of irons.
Aprés cure lou leu de farine de veces avec miel et autres cures tant qu’il soit saneis.	After curing the limb with flour and honey, and other treatments until it is healed.
Quant enfleure vient en aucun membre et est curee par medicines et oiles et emplastres, et il n’est mie sanez, adonques li fai cauteres sus le membre selonc la grandour et la petitece dou membre; et soit li cauteres un poc entrans en l’espés dou keur; puis le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	When inflammation comes to any limb and is treated with medicines, oils, and plasters, and it is not healed, then you do cauterization above the limb according to its length and width; and let the cauterization be a little inside the edge of the wound; then treat the pain until it is healed.
Et aucune fois fait on cautere et a la main et au piet et au dos, a l’issue dou nerf que muet le membre, et ensi si est ostee li enfleure; et toutevoie ne s’en entremette nuls s’il n’est conoissans des membres et des issues des ners movans lou cors.	And never performed fire cauterization by hand and on the back and at the base of the nerve that paralyzes the limb, and thus if it is set, it becomes inflamed; and in any case, no one interferes unless they are knowledgeable about the members and their issues moving the body.
de albaras	I'm sorry, I don't understand your request
Quant li maladie qui est apelee «albaras» est enveillie, et li engien de medicine n’i valent rien, adonques le cauterize d’un cautere un poc parfont, selonc la quantiteit de l’espés dou keur, tant que li blenchour soit ostee, et soit muee sa color; puis le cure de farine de veces et de lentilles avec oile roset et foilles de plantain, et sanc de colon et sanc d’alondre, de chescun une partie; et soit mellez tout ensamble, et soit liiez d’un drapel, et soit aers au leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	When the disease called "albaras" is awake, and the medical art does not help, then cauterize with a cautery a little in front, according to the quantity of the courage, until the blench is set, and its color is restored; then treat with flour and lentils with rose oil and plantain leaves, and salt of colon and salt of almond, each part; and mix everything together, and apply it to the wound, and cover it with a cloth, and keep it on the body until it is healed.
li cure de chancre par cautere	The treatment of chancre by cauterization
Quant chancre vient au comencement, et tu lou vues arrester, si le cauterize au cautere qui semble I cercle, tout entor au tour dou chancre.	When chancre first appears and you cannot stop its spread, then cauterize it with a cauterizing iron shaped like a circle around the entire edge of the chancre.
Et toutevoie li saige dirent que on faice cautere ausi au mileu dou chancre; et toutevoie ceu ne me semble mie boin, car je redous que il ne soit ulcerez et corrumpus, et je l’ai ja veut avenir aucune fois; et plus droituriere chose est qu’il soit cauteriés entor, au cautere qui est apelez «circule», si com nos avons dit en mout de cauteres.	And all the wise say that one should also make a cauterization in the middle of the chancre; and I do not think it is good because I believe it will not become ulcerated and corrupted, and I have never seen it happen once; and a more important thing is that it be cauterized around, with the cauterizing iron called "circle", as we have said in many cauterizations.
de l’enfleure qui ne puet meurer	of the swelling that cannot die
Quant aucuns ait une maladie qui est apelee «adubelati», et elle tarde de meurer ou por la superfluiteit qu’ele fait ou por l’eaige dou malaide quant il est decrepites (c’est a dire trop vielz) et il a poc de sanc, ou por lou tens; et tu la vues haster de meurer: adonques le cauterize entor de mout de petis cauteres en poignant; aprés le laisse ensi.	When anyone has a disease called "adubelati", and it takes a long time to die or due to the excess it causes or due to the age of the patient when they are very old and have little blood, or due to the tension; then you see it hastening to die: therefore cauterize around with many small cauteries pricking; afterwards leave it like this.
Car elle se hastera de meureir.	For it will hasten to die.
Et se tu la vues percier a tout le cautere, si chaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	And if you see it pierce through all the cauterization, then heat the cauterization from where this is the form:
Et met ta main en mileu de cele maladie qui est apellee «adubelati» tant que li cauteres ait perciet lou keur, et soit telz li cauteres que li malaides lou sente defuers en teil maniere que li cours de la porriture soit alegis.	And place your hand in the middle of this disease called "adubelati" until the cauteries have pierced through, and be such cauteries that the hairs feel afterwards in a similar manner as the course of the pustule is alleviated.
Aprés le cure tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	After the treatment until they are completely healed.
li cure dou feu par fer	The treatment of fire by iron.
Une autre maniere de maladie i a qui est apelee «corrodens», et n’est autre chose que une mengeson de membre, car ele menjut les membres ausi com li feus les leignes seches.	Another way of disease is called "corrodens", and it is nothing but a small amount of member, for it bends the members as if the dry reeds.
Se tu vois ceste maladie en leu qui puisse soffrir cautere ensamble feu, adonques eschaufe les cauteres clavile mout petit et grant, selonc ceu qu’il covient au leu ou li maladie est; aprés le cauterize de toutes pars tant que tu erraiche toute la corruption, et nen remaigne rien de li, que tout ceu qui est corrumpus ne soit osteit.	If you see this disease in the limb that can suffer cauterization together with fire, then heat the cauteries clavile very small and great, according to what is needed for the limb or the disease; after cauterizing all parts until you reach all the corruption, and nothing remains of it, so that all that is corrupted is removed.
Et puis le laisse III jors, et met sus les leus cauterizez soffre broiet avec oile tant que les eschaudures dou feu soient ostees, et toute li corruption.	And then leave it for three days, and apply the cauterized ointment on the wounds with oil until the scabs from the fire are removed and all corruption.
Aprés lou cure d’oignemens engendrans char.	After the treatment of burns, char.
Et se tu vois aprés III jors que chars saine ne naisse, c’est boin; et se ceu non, si rencomence le cautere sus ceu qui est demoreit des leus corrumpus.	And if you see after three days that healthy char does not grow, it is good; and if not, then restart the cauterization on the remaining corruption.
Et ceste mengeson est aucune fois esteit curee de medicine ague en leu de cautere de feu; mais toutevoie cautere de feu est de plus grant aide, et j’ai ja dit la cure de la medicine ague en la division: pren la quant tu en as mestier.	And this method has never been cured by medical ointment in the place of fire cauterization; but fire cauterization is always greater help, and I have already told the cure of the medical ointment in the division: take it when you have need.
des porrelz qui vienent as piez	of the broken bones that come from the feet
Mout de fois avient que as piez par defuers naist une maladie qui est apelee «clos» selonc nostre entencion, et est une grosse chose fautree qui blece lou piet.	often from the feet comes a disease called "closed" according to our understanding, and is a great thing that causes the foot to swell greatly.
Et li cauteres de ceste maladie si est selonc II manieres.	And the cauteries of this disease are according to two methods.
C’est a savoir cautere de feu, et cautere d’aigue chaude.	That is to say, fire cauterization and water-hot cauterization.
Cautere de feu si est que tu eschaufe I cautere cheveit ausi com est une penne de vouteul, et soit fait de boin fer a la mesure qu’il puisse porpenre le clou de toutes pars, et qu’il i ait subtilz marges; aprés le met tout chaut sus lou clou, et torne ta main tot entor le clou tant qu’il viegne au font dou clou; et lou laisse ensi III jors tant qu’il encomence giter porriture; puis li fai un emplaustre de malves savaiges broiies avec seil, et laisse l’emplaustre sus toute la nuit, et li clous cherra et sera desracinez de ses racines.	Fire cauterization is that you heat the cauterizer like a pen of quill, and it is made of good iron at the measure that it can penetrate the nail from all parts, and that it has thin edges; afterwards, put it all hot on top of the nail, and turn your hand all around the nail until it reaches the bottom of the nail; and leave it thus for three days until it begins to rot; then make an ointment of wild herbs crushed with oil, and leave the ointment all night, and the nail will close and be removed from its roots.
Puis cure le leu d’oignement enjanrant char tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then treat the limb with heat until it is healed.
Et s’il sont convertit par defuers lou cors, et maintes fois avient et en mains et em piez, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere d’aigue chaude; et est en teil maniere: pren une cainne d’arain ou de fer, ou une penne de vouteul, et met sus lou clou et l’althelul, c’est asavoir porrelz verrues; et met la cainne sus si qu’ele porpreigne tout entor, puis i met un poc d’awe chaude, et retien bien ta main, et presse ta main en tornant si que li marge de la cainne viegne a la racine dou clou, et puisse trover l’aigue chaude voie parfonde jusc’a la racine; et soffre li malaides un poc la mordication de l’aigue chaude une houre; puis le laisse ensi, et il se derracinera tous a tout ses racines.	And if they are converted by the body's heat, and often in hands and feet, it is necessary to cauterize with hot iron; and it is done in this way: take a needle of iron or steel, or a quill pen, and place it on the nail and the cuticle, that is to say, the skin around the nail; then put a little hot water, and hold your hand firmly, and press your hand so that the edge of the needle comes to the root of the nail, and find the hot water penetrating deeply up to the root; and suffer the pain of the hot water for one hour; then leave it thus, and it will all fall off at its roots.
Ensi fai un aprés autre, tant que tu esraiches toz ces qui sont au cors, puis les cure des oignemens qui engenrent char.	Then do another one, until you have removed all those that are in the body, then cure the wounds that entangle the heart.
li cure dou trembler	the treatment of trembling
Quant aucuns tremble de froidor de ners, ou de fievre quartaine ou d’autre, si covient que tu li faices IIII cauteres ou IV sus l’espinee dou dos, I cautere entre chescune espinee; et I cautere ou pez, et I sus l’estomac au cautere olivaire; si laissera lou trembler, et se hastera li santez de la maladie froide.	When anyone trembles from cold or from a quarter fever or other, it is necessary that you make four cautery burns or four above the spine of the back; one cautery between each spine; and one on the chest, and one above the stomach at the cauterizing olive; this will allow them to tremble, and will hasten the healing of the disease.
des pustules puans	of pus-filled blisters
Aucune fois apperent par defuers le cors bathes, ou pustules puans, que vienent de grosses matieres corrumpues.	No matter how often the body is washed, or the pustules are popped that come from large, corrupting matters.
si covient au premier quant eles apperent que on faice cautere sus chescun chief de la pustule: un cautere subtil de fust de mirte, de coi li pointe soit emprise au feu, ou de racine de aristologe longe, ou au cautere lenticulaire.	If it is necessary when they appear that a fire cautery be performed on each pustule head: a subtle fire cautery from a twig of mugwort, of which the point is grasped in the fire, or from the root of aristolochia, or with a lenticular cauterizer.
Et aucune fois les cauterize on au comencement quant il aperent, selonc ceste maniere, et il ne puent croistre des enqui en avant, mais est desrompue li superfluitez dont il vienent, et sont sanez; mais il covient que ceu soit fait aprés l’evacuation de sanc.	And no matter how often they are cauterized at the beginning when they appear, in this manner, and it cannot grow again, but is broken up from the excess from which they come, and are healed; but it is necessary that this be done after the evacuation of blood.
quant li artere est copee	when the artery is cut
Maintes fois avient grans decorremens de sanc de l’artere qui est copee a la plaie que vient au pardefuers, ou a l’incision de l’aposteme, ou au cautere dou membre, et as semblans choses; et est mout grief chose d’estenchier.	often there is great bleeding from the artery that is cut at the wound that comes from the sides, or at the incision of the abscess, or in the cauterization of the member, and similar things; and it is a very difficult thing to stop.
Et toutevoie quant ceu avient a aucun, si te haste de mettre ton doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne, et l’estrain mout tant que li sans soit apaisiez desoz ton doi, et que goute n’en isse plus; puis met au feu les cauteres olivaire plusors petis et grans tant qu’il soient tuit rouge; puis empren I, ou grant ou petit selonc la plaie et lou leu en coi li artere est route, et met le cautere sus cele voine ou tu tiens ton doi, et tien le cautere tant sus que li sans soit restainchiez.	And in any case when this happens to anyone, you must quickly place your finger on the wound of the vein, and press very hard until the bleeding is stopped and no more blood comes out; then put the cauteries of olive oil several times, both small and large, as long as they are all red; then apply I, or a great or little one according to the wound and the limb in which the artery is severed, and place the cautery on that vein where you hold your finger, and keep the cautery there until the bleeding is stopped.
Et s’il saut fuers quant tu lieves ton doi desus la voinne, et li cauteres estint, si pren hastivement I autre des cauteres qui sont au feu.	And if the first one you lift above the vein, and the cauteries are extinguished, then quickly take the other cauteries that are in the fire.
Et ne cesser de faire ceu l’un aprés l’autre tant que li sans soit estenchiez; et warde que tu n’ardes lou nerf qui est delez, et que autre malice ne viegne sus lou malaide; et saiches que quant sans decourt de l’artere, c’on ne lou puet mie bien restenchier meismement quant li artere est grans, se ceu n’est par une des IIII manieres que nos avons dit: ou par cautere, ou par extraction quant ele n’est mie traite, ou par fort liement de fil, ou par medicines mises sus qui ont pooir de restenchier sanc; et soit liee et estrainte avennament.	And do not cease to apply them one after the other until the wound is cleansed; and be careful not to burn the nerve that is nearby, and that no other harm comes over the wound; and be sure that when the artery is not cut, it cannot be properly stopped immediately if the artery is large, unless by one of the four methods we have mentioned: or by cauterization, or by extraction when it is not yet treated, or by a strong thread, or by medicines placed on top which have power to stop bleeding; and let it be tied and pressed.
Qui i amenistrera restenchement de liier estroitement de drapelz ou de metre choses ardans sus, ou autres semblans choses, se n’i profite se poc non.	Whoever administers the tightening of knots closely with cloth or metal things burning above, or other similar things, does not benefit unless they do not.
Et se ce avient a aucun et il n’ait mie mire ne medicine present, si doit mettre son doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne si com nos avons dit, et bien estrendre tant qu’il soit restenchiez desus la plaie et desus la voinne; et ne remuer lou doit, mais lou moille d’awe froide sovent que soit mout froide tant que li sans soit congelez et engrossiez et restenchiez; et faice des enqui en avant ceu dont il a mestier de cauteres et de medicines.	And if this happens to anyone and they do not have any medicine present, they should place their little finger index above the wound of the vein as we have said, and well tighten until it is tightened above the wound and above the vein; and they should not move it, but they should rub it with cold water often until it is very cold so that the wound does not freeze and swell up and tighten; and make inquiries about what they need for cauterizing and medicines.
Ci encomence li secons livre des cures de taille	Here begins the second book of the cures of tails
Nos vos avons dit ou premier chapistre toute maladie en coi il covient cautere de feu, ou de medicine ardans, et les oquisons et les causes et les estrumens et les formes des cauteres; et ai mis celui chapistre des lou chief jusc’a piez, et je irai en cest chapistre par celi meisme voie por ceu c’on trueve plus legierement ceu c’on voura.	We have told you in the first chapter of all diseases where it is necessary to cauterize with fire or burning medicine, and the conditions and causes and instruments and forms of the cauteries; and I will put this chapter about the lower limb from head to foot, and I will go into this chapter by that same way so that we can find more easily what we want.
Et ainsois que je encomence ceu, il covient, chier fil, que vos aprenez que en cest chapistre a plus de peril et de paor que ou premier des cauteres, et por ceu il covient plus grant cautele.	And therefore when I begin this chapter, it is necessary, dear child, that you learn that in this chapter there is more danger and fear than in the first of the cauteries, and for this reason it is necessary to take greater care.
Car en l’ovraige de cest chapistre avient maintes fois evacuation de sanc a l’ovrir la voinne, et a l’incision sus aposteme, et as cures des plaies, et a l’estraction des saiettes, et a l’incision sus la piere, et les semblans choses; ou il a doutance et paor, et en vient li mors a plusors.	For in the work of this chapter, there is often the evacuation of blood when opening a vein, and incising an abscess, and in the treatment of wounds, and in the extraction of arrows, and in cutting into stones, and similar things; where there is doubt and fear, and many die.
Et je vos amoneste que vos n’entreprenez folie.	And I warn you not to undertake folly.
Car mout de manieres de gens vienent en cures.	For many ways of people come in cures.
si vienent de telz qui s’aïrent si avec lor maladie qu’il muerent legierement por la forsenerie qu’il trueve de sa maladie, et de la grandour de son malice; et de ces doit on avoir paor.	if they come from such people who are so with their disease that they die immediately because of the harm they receive from their disease, and the greatness of its malice; and of these one must have fear.
Et de ces i a qui te done son sens, et dit: «atendez, je sui garis»; et li maladie est despitouse.	And of these, there are those who give you their sense, and say: "Wait, I am in pain"; and the illness is spiteful.
Il ne covient mie que vos vos consentez a ces qui vienent a vos qui ont ceste maniere, mais mettez plus grant cusanson en vostre honor qu’en vostre covoitise, et n’ovrez mie folement mais saigement de ceu dont vos estes certain, et dont vos poez avoir pris et los; et usez de pronostication et de indication en cures de vos malaides a coi salus soit convertie; et ceu vos aidera a aquester bone renommee, et gloire, et memoire de loenge.	It is not necessary to grant permission to those who come to you who have this manner, but put greater caution in your honor than in your desire, and do not open foolishly but wisely of that of which you are certain, and which you have taken and lost; and use prediction and indication in the treatment of your ills for health to be converted; and this will help you to acquire good reputation, and glory, and memory for long.
Tres chier fil, Nostres Sires vos doint boin entendement et droiture, et se vos vuelle espireir de la sainte inspiration de sa main, amen.	Very dear son, Our Lords give you good understanding and justice, and if you wish to breathe from the holy inspiration of his hand, indeed.
Or je vos ai ordeneit cest chapistre en devisant par chapistres, selonc ceu qu’il est devant ou chapistre des cauteres, que je vos ai deviseit des le chief jusc’a piez, por ceu que vos trovez plus legierement ceu dont vos avrez mestier.	I have ordered you to this chapter by advising from other chapters, according to what it is before or a chapter of cauteries, that I have advised from the beginning to the end, so that you find it more easily what you will have to do.
dou chief plein d’aigue	the beginning full of sharp
Saiches que ceste maladie vient mout de fois as enfans a l’enfanter, et quant li baille estraint trop fort le chief de l’enfant; et aucune fois vient ceu de cause reponue que on ne seit.	This disease comes often to children at birth, and when the midwife presses too hard on the child's head; and sometimes it comes because of a repelled cause that one is not.
Et je ne vis onques ceste maladie fuers qu’en enfans, et a toz ces que j’ai veus se hastait li mors; et por ceu me semble qu’il me vaut mues lassier l’ovraige en teilz cures.	And I have never seen this disease except in children, and to all those that I have seen it was fatal; and therefore it seems to me that it is better to avoid the work in such treatments.
Et je vis I enfant de coi li chiés estoit plains d’aigue, et li chief engroissoit chescun jor tant qu’il ne lou pooit sostenir; et crut tant li moistor qu’il fut mors, et ceste moistor si est assemblee desoz l’os sus lou syphac, entre lou keur et l’os; et li ovraiges si est telz se li moistor est entre lou keur et l’os, et li apostemes est petis, que tu fendes emmi lou chief une fendure large; et soit ausi longe com II nous, tant que li mostor corre; et vez ci la forme dou spatumile:	I saw a child who was complaining of severe pain in the shoulder, and the head was swelling each day until it could no longer bear it; and he thought so much of the moisture that he died, and this moisture is gathered outside the bone above the shoulder joint, between the skin and the bone; and the procedures are such that if the moisture is between the skin and the bone, and the abscesses are small, you should make a wide cut in the head; and it should be as long as twice our finger, so that the moisture flows out; and take the shape of the space:
Se li moistor est plus creue, et li aposteme soit plus grans, si fai II fendures en maniere d’une croix, selonc ceste forme:	If the moisture is more extensive, and the abscess is larger, then make two cuts in the shape of a cross, according to this form:
Et se li moistor est desoz l’os, et li signes que tu vois les commissures dou chief overtes de chescune partie, et li aigue saut fuer quant tu la presses de ta main au dedens, et ceu ne t’est mie reponut: si covient que tu fendes enmi lou chief III fendures selonc ceste maniere:	And if the moisture is under the bone, and the signs you see are the commissures of the joint opening on each part, and the sharp pain when you press it with your hand from inside, and it does not return: then you must make three cuts in the head like this:
Et aprés l’incision estrai la moistor toute fuers.	And after the incision, remove all the moisture.
Aprés estraint les fendures de drapelz et de poudres, et i met vin et oile, et laisse ensi jusc’a cinquieme jor; puis le deslie, et cure la plaie par tentes et par oignemens, et laisse estraindre le chief egaument, et done mengier au malaide viande seche de poc de moistor tant que li membre soit confortez et sanez.	After straining the cuts with cloths and powders, and putting in wine and oil, leave it thus for five days; then remove it, and treat the wound with tents and counter-irritants, and keep the shoulder strained evenly, and gradually introduce dry food without moisture until the member is comfortable and healthy.
Et une autre maniere d’incision est que tu regardes ou apert li grandor de l’aposteme, et li assemblé de l’aigue; car aucune fois est elle devant; aucune fois derrier; aucune fois en destre; et aucune fois en senestre.	Another method of incision is to look at the size of the abscess and the angle of the needle; for it is never in front, never behind, never on the right side, and never on the left side.
Taille donques lai ou li aposteme apert, et l’emplissement de l’aigue, et lou fent selonc ce que tu en as le pooir; et warde que tu ne coper l’artere; et veigne flun de sanc, si que li malaides muere dou decorrement de sanc et de l’evacuation de moistor.	Therefore, open the abscess and fill the needle, and make the cut according to what you can do; and be careful not to cover the artery; and if blood flows, it can cause the wounds to die due to the flow of blood and the evacuation of moisture.
de reume	to return
Quant il avient a aucun une maladie qui est apelee «catarre» as eulz ou au pis, et li maladie est anciainne, et li cure de medicine ne profite mie, adonques li derraine cure si est li cauteres avec ceu c’on li copera les II arteres.	When it comes to a certain disease called "cataract" in the eyes or on the pupil, and the disease is ancient, and the medical treatment does not help much, then the cure is to cauterize with what is used to cover the two arteries.
Il covient donques, cant tu les vues coper, que li malaides faice rere son chief; aprés li frotte lou leu d’un drapel aspre tant que les arteres aperent, puis estraingne li malaides son col a tout I drapel; puis regarde ou li voine bait, et li leus de l’une et de l’autre sont aprés les oreilles, et poc sont reponues; puis signe les leus d’enche, puis cope l’une et l’autre d’un spatumile agut de II pars, tant que li taille veigne jusc’a l’os, et ceu soit par lou large dou chief.	Therefore, when you see the hairs growing long and even, it is necessary to let them grow until they reach their full length; then rub the skin with a rough cloth until the arteries are visible, then pull back the hair on the entire cloth; then look where the blood flows, and the veins on both sides of the ear are usually close together, and then place a bandage over them; then sign the bandages at the same spot, then cut both with a sharp knife until the wound comes just short of the bone, and this should be done carefully to avoid injuring the skull.
Et se tu vues, boute le spatumile desoz l’artere et la cope au desus, en taillant ausi com II dois au traver.	And if you see, push the sharp knife away from the artery and cut above it, as you would through the skin.
Et quant li voinne est copee, si saut li sans en haut continuelment fuers.	And when the vein is cut, then continuously pour water from above.
Et se li artere n’apert au sentir, si covient que tu mesures la quantiteit de l’espaice de III dois, puis seigne d’enche et fent jusc’a l’os; et ceu qu’il covient dou sanc mettre fuers si est VI c/, et par aventure un poc plus ou moins, selonc ce que li malaides puet soffrir, et la repletion de l’artere; puis regarde la plaie: s’il remaint sus l’os point dou syphac, si le cope que apostemes chaus n’i veigne, puis estrain la plaie et lie, et la cure d’oignement tant qu’ele soit sanee.	And if the artery does not open at first feeling, then measure the quantity of the space of three fingers, then sign it and apply it to the bone; and what is needed for the arrow is six centimeters, and perhaps a little more or less, depending on how much the wound can bear, and the replacement of the artery; then look at the wound: if it remains above the bone point, if the coping that we apply does not come out, then cover the wound and tie, and the ointment cure until it is healed.
de emigrainne	of the shoulder
Quant emigrainne anciaine vient, et catarre agut, por les moistors des larmes et les chalors en temples et sode anciene forsenee et semblans choses, et il est medicinez par manieres de cures de medicine et tout ceu ne li profite mie, si estraions les arteres des temples et lou cauterizons, si com nos avons conteit.	When the ancient shoulder ailment comes, and the fire cauterization is not effective due to the moisture of tears and the heat in the temples and the old age and similar things, and it is treated by means of medical cures and nothing helps him, then we must cauterize the arteries of the temples and do as we have told.
Et li maniere de l’estraction d’elles si est que li malaides faice rere les poilz de ses temples, et entende a l’artere qui apert en la temple, car elle apert bien par son batement, et est poc reponue fuers que en aucuns homes qui sont trop froit; et s’elle est reponue, si estraigne son col li malaides d’aucuns drapelz, puis frote le leu d’aucun aspre drap, et arose le leu d’aigue chaude tant que li artere apere manifestement; puis pren le spatumile de coi ci est li forme:	And the method of extracting them is that the hairs of his temples should be made to face backward, and he should listen to the artery which opens in the temple, because it opens well by its beating, and it is not restored until in some men who are too cold; and if it is restored, then one should strain the skin with some cloths, then rub the skin with any rough cloth, and heat the skin with hot water until the artery appears clearly; then take the spatula of which this is the shape:
puis escorche le cuir legierement tant que tu veignes a l’artere, puis la trai en haut as pinceures, et la depart bien des toiles que sont desoz li de chescune partie; et se li artere est subtilz, si la torne a la pointe de l’uncine, puis la cope de celle partie selonc la quantiteit des II chiés.	Then slightly scrape the light skin until you reach the artery, then cut it upwards with pincers, and pull out several threads that are stuck to each part; and if the artery is thin, turn it to the tip of the needle, then cover that part according to the amount of the two chapters.
Car s’elle n’est copee, si ne saut mie li sans dou tout en tout.	But if it is not covered, it will not heal at all.
Et trai dou sanc des VI c/, jusc’a III; et se li artere est grans, si covient que tu la lies en II leus d’un fil double fort de soie, que porriture n’i veigne devant le soudement de la plaie, et veigne decorremens de sanc; puis cope la superfluiteit qui est entre les II liiens en celle houre meisme, et puis, se tu vues, si lou cauterize dou cautere cutellaire jusc’a l’os tant que li chiés soient copez; et c’est li muedre oevre, se li malaides n’a fievre et il est de chaude complexion.	And draw out blood from the sixth chamber to the third; and if the artery is large, it is necessary that you tie it in two lengths of a strong silk thread, which does not allow any blood to come before the scab of the wound, and comes out as clots of blood; then cover the excess that is between the two threads in the same hour, and then, if you see, if the fire cauterizes the cutellaire cautery up to the bone until the chapters are covered; and this is the final work, if the wounds do not have fever and he is of hot constitution.
Car li cauteres est aide por finir les moistors: por ceu est il de plus grant aide as moistors.	For the fire cautery, it is used to finish off moistures: because it is the greatest help against moistures.
Ou il covient por l’estraction des arteres que om emplisse lou leu de viel coton et mette on sus tentes bien faites; et quant on les desliera, si soit curez de medicines seches que font naistre char, et de tentes, tant qu’il soit sanez; et se sans cort de l’artere tant dis com tu i oevres, si te haste dou coper par cautere, ou tu emple lou leu de vitriole et l’estrain a ta main que li sans soit estainchiez; et se tu n’as ceu present, si met sor le leu ton doit tant que li sans soit congelez, et arose le leu d’aigue froide tant que li sans cesse, et soit estraint si com il covient; et ceu qui est muedre et plus legier en l’estraction de l’artere est que tu cauterizes la voinne de cest cautere trenchant de II pars, mais li trenchant soient bien espés por warder plus longement lor chalor.	When it is necessary for the extraction of arteries, one should fill the wound with old cotton and place dry bandages on top; and when they are removed, care should be taken with dry medicines that make charcoal and bandages until they are healed; and if there is no court of the artery, as much as you can work, then hasten to cover it with fire cautery, or fill the wound with vitriol and strain it to your hand so that the wound does not become stained; and if you do not have this present, then place ice on the wound until the wound is congealed, and raise the wound with boiling hot water until it is stopped, and keep it as it should be; and what is more difficult and lighter in the extraction of the artery is that you cauterize the vein with this cautery cutting from II parts, but the cuts should be well spaced to last longer.
Car quant li estrumens est trop tenves, si tient moins sa chalor.	When the instrument is too tight, it holds less heat.
Et doit avoir entre les II coutelz I doit de gros d’espaice, et puis quant tu as signiet d’enche les II leus, et tu mes lou fer ardant sus tant qu’il viegne jusc’a l’os, et cope la voinne en II leus; et soient esloigniet entre les II chiés car il n’est mie soudez de cest cautere dou tout en tout; et c’est li forme dou cautere:	And it should have between the two knives a gap of large space, and then when you have inserted the two blades, and you melt the hot iron above until it comes near the bone, and cover the vein in two places; and they should be separated between the two cuts because there is no surety of this cauterization at all; and this is the form of the cauterization:
des larmes	of tears
Quant les larmes des eulz sont dessendans des voinnes que sont sus lou test dou chief de fuer, et il ne profite mie cure de medicine c’on i faice, et tu vois la faice dou malaide enrougir, et sent ou front ambulation si com de fremis; et sui oil sont tenve et moiste si que li poil des papieres sont cheut, et sont eschaufees les papieres, et escorchies de l’ardor des larmes, si ait mestier de ceste cure.	When the tears of the eyes are dripping from veins that are above the surface of the chief of the forehead, and it does not improve with any medicine, and you see the face of the pain twisted, and it feels like a tremor; and they are held and moist so that the hairs of the eyelashes are soaked, and the eyelashes are curled, and scorched by the heat of the tears, if there is a need for this cure.
Et l’apelerent li ancien «cure contuse», et est que tu faices a rere au malaide qui a ceste maladie les poilz qu’il ait ou front, puis li fai III fendures ou front igalment selonc la longesce dou front; et soit l’une des fendures ausi com II doi tout emmi lou front en avalant aval jusc’a neif, et les autres II as II costelz par desus les papieres, et te garde de l’incision des arteres que sont as II costez par desus les papieres; et aloigne ta main de la continuation des II mandibules, et soit chescune plaie la quantiteit de III dois au traver joins; et aies apparillie une piece d’esponge et mout de drapelz ses por essuer lou sanc, puis boute le spatumile agut de II pars de coi ci est li forme:	And they called the ancient "wound healer," and you should apply pressure to the painful part that has this disease, whether it is front or back, then make three cuts equally long according to the length of the front; and one of the cuts as two teeth down from the front in descending, and the others two on each side of the ribs, and beware of the incision of the arteries that are on each side of the ribs; and keep your hand away from the continuation of the two mandibles, and for each wound the quantity of three doses through the joins; and have prepared a piece of sponge and much cloth to soak up the blood, then stop the bleeding with the shape of this:
des l’incision qui est dever la temple jusc’a la seconde incision; et escorche tout le keur qui est entre les II fendures a tot lou syfac qui est sus l’os, puis fai autreteil des la moiene incision jusc’a l’autre seconde, et puis estrai fuer cest spatumile.	From the incision that is made from the temple down to the second incision; and scrape off all the skin that is between the two cuts up to the surface of the bone, then make another incision from the other side of the same incision to the other second, and then extract this piece of bone.
si boute en la premiere fendure l’estrument qui est apelez «cultellaire», et est tresbien trenchans d’une part, et d’autre part est souef, ne mie trenchans, et c’est li forme:	If you put the tool called "curette" in the first incision, it is very sharp on one side and blunt on the other, and this is its shape:
Et met le costeit taillant vers la char aerse au keur, et lou costeit souef vers l’os, et lou boute tant qu’il veigne a la moiene fendure.	And place the sharp edge of the tool towards the bone and the blunt side towards the skin, and scrape until it reaches the same incision.
Et cope toz les vasselz que dessendent dou chief as eulz tant que l’incision soit continue jusc’a ceu qui apert dou keur, et puis autreteil fai en la moiene fendure jusc’a l’autre defuer; et puis estrai dou sanc igalment, et espresse lou leu por le sanc pris; puis met en chescune fendure une tente de viel coton, et met sus drapelz moilliez en vin et en oile et en aisil, et garde que apostemes chaus n’i veigne; et au tier jor deslie lou liien, et i amenistre grant planteit d’aigue tede, puis lou cure d’oignement basilicon avec oile roset, et d’autres cures dont on cure plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And for all the vessels that descend from the head as far as the eyes until the incision is continuous to the depth where the knife opens, and then make another one in the same wound towards the other side; and then extract the arrow evenly, and express the blood from the wound taken; then put a tent of old cotton in each wound, and put on dressings moistened with wine and oil and vinegar, and guard that abscesses do not come; and for the wound, apply a great deal of vinegar, then the ointment basilicon with rose oil, and other cures to heal wounds, as long as they are healed.
dou reume des eulz	The return of the eyes
Quant a aucun vienent catarre agut acostumeement, et tu vois les eulz tenves et petis, et afoiblir la veue, et les papieres brulees; et li poil chieent, et ou chief en parfont a dolor ague, et li malaides esternue; adonques saiches par ces accidens que celles matieres et cil catharre ne vient fuer que de maintes voines, et li muedre cure que i est, si est ceste.	When anyone comes for the operation of cautery, and you see the eyes tight and small, and weakened vision, and the papers burned; and the hairs are shaved, and the pain in the forehead is great, and the eyelashes are out; then by these accidents that those matters and that cautery do not come but from many wounds, and the patient's condition that there is, if this is.
Et est que tu comande au malaide a rere son front, puis fai une grant fendure emmi lou front, et une autre dou large I poc.	And it is that you command the patient to turn his head back, then make a great cut through the forehead, and another wide at the top of the nose.
Et comence des la fendure de la temple senestre a la temple destre, et soit li incision jusc’a l’os; et esloigne ta main des ners des temples que muevent au mengier; et quant li os est descovers, si essue tout le sanc a une esponge, et puis desevre entre les II levres de la fendure et i met coton viel, et tentes de lin; puis lie desus drapelz moilliez en vin et en oile, et te garde d’aposteme chaut; quant il est ostez, si covient que tu frottes l’os tant que chars i comence a naistre, puis le cure de choses exiccatives, que font enjanrer char.	And from the wound on the right temple to the left temple, and let the incision be just to the bone; and keep your hand away from the nerves of the temples that move in the mouth; and when the bone is exposed, suck out all the blood with a sponge, then clean between the two lips of the wound and put on cotton and linen; then cover with moistened cloths mixed with wine and oil, and guard against abscess forming; when it is removed, it is necessary to rub the bone until charred begins to form, then care for things that cause healing, like honey.
En teil maniere: pren II parties de flor de froment, et de colofoine IIII parties, et en fai emplaustre; et l’aministre en ces plaies por enjanrer char per tout.	In this manner: Take two parts of wheat flour and four parts of mustard, and make a poultice; and apply it to these wounds to draw out the char perforce throughout.
de l’estoupement des oreilles	of the dizziness of the ears
Tout ceu que chiet ens oreilles est une des IIII choses: ou grains, ou beste, ou piere de mine ou semblans chose si com fer; ou semence, si com jaisses, feves, pois; ou chose defluans si com aigue et aisilz et semblans choses.	All that which goes into the ears is one of the four things: grains, beasts, stones or similar things like iron; seeds, such as grapes, beans, and peas; or things flowing such as sharp and smooth things and similar things.
Quant il chiet en l’oreille piere ou autre maniere de chose que ne s’ajoste mie a l’oreille, ne ne croist en l’oreille, si met l’oreille au solel.	When it goes into the ear as a stone or other similar thing that does not fit well in the ear, it does not grow in the ear, so put the ear to the sunlight.
Se tu vois la piere, si distille aucun poc d’oile violet ou oile de sisament, puis i amenistre extraction; et lou fai esternuer de condisi, et li estoupe les narines quant li esternuemens vient, et met entor l’oreille pieces de drapelz ou laine; et estent l’oreille au desus.	If you see the arrow, if any drop of violet or fennel oil drips, then relieve extraction; and the effect is to sneeze out conditions, and when sneezing comes, cover the nose, and put pieces of cloth or wool around the ear; and hold the ear upwards.
Mout de fois vient fuer par ceste cure; et s’elle ne vient fuer, se li amenistre extraction as pinceures subtilz, de coi ci est li forme:	Often this treatment causes vomiting; and if it does not cause vomiting, then relieve extraction with subtle pins of this form.
S’elle saut fuer as pinceures, c’est boin; se ceu non, si amenistre extraction a l’oncine subtil de petite doubleure; et s’elle ne saut par ceu, si fai une caine d’arain et boute lou chief de la cainne ou pertuis de l’oreille fort, et estoupe ceu qui est entor la cainne de cire mole si que li vens n’i puisse entrer avec la cainne; puis le trai fuer forment, car mout de fois vient fuer si com nos avons dit; et s’elle ne vient fuer en teil maniere, si prent glut de coi en prent les oisiaus, et met en som aucun estrument qui soit a point por ceu faire, et met un poc de coton entor; puis presse le glut sus la piere ou quel chose que ce soit, et trai fuer. et amenistre incision de celui grain.	and make an incision of that small one.

s’elle saut fuer per ceu, c’est boin.	If it jumps out because of the heat, that's good.

de l’estoupement des oreilles	of ear obstruction
Aucun enfant naissent qui n’ont nul pertus ens oreilles; et ceste meisme chose avient as homes par estoupement de plaie, ou de char nee dedens l’oreille, et cist estoupemens vient aucune fois em parfont en l’oreille, si c’on ne lou puet veoir; et aucune fois avient I poc defuer lou pertus, et lou voit om bien. de la char des papieres	of the writing of papers
Cist althelul que vienent em papieres des eulz quant ils sont moiste et sont sec, si covient que tu les estendes de tenailles et de pinceures, et le cope d’un spatumile de ses racines; puis met sor le leu vitriole broiet.	This is the method for removing thorns from papers when they are wet and dry: spread them out with tongs and pincers, and remove the roots of their points; then place them on a lead plate of its base.
Et se sans en decort, si le cauterize dou cautere lenticulaire subtil, et li cauterizeir aprés l’incision vaut mues; et maintes fois repairent, cant aucune chose demoure de lor racines; et quant elles sont cauterizees par feu, si sont arses celles racines et ne revienent mie. de la gresle	of the sand
Maintes fois vienent em papieres des eulz unes choses que semblent gresle en sa forme et en sa duresce, et por ceu est ceste maladie apelee «grandine», et est une assemblee de moistor grosse en la papiere desus et desoz; li ovraiges est telz: pren warde se li grandine se muet d’une part et d’autre, et c’est legiere chose a savoir; fent la donques dou large, puis l’escorche de chescune partie legierement, puis la prent as pinceures, et la cope.	Frequently, in papers, there are things that seem to be gritty in their form and hardness, and because of this disease is called "hail," and it is an assembly of moisture large on the paper above and below; the work is as follows: if the hail moves from one side to another, it is a light thing to know; then make it wide, then scrape each part lightly, then take it with pincers, and the cover.
se tu ne la pues coper sens percier un poc la papiere, si ne grieve rien au malaide; et se li fendure est grans, si l’assemble a une costure, et la cure tant qu’ele soit sanee; et s’elle est petite, si n’i faire point de force, car li oignemens la restoure tantost et enjanre char.	If you do not cover it with a small puncture in the paper, it does not hurt the patient; and if the force is great, it assembles at a seam, and the cure until it is healthy; and if it is small, do not make any force, for the wounds will restore quickly and inflame.

And if the splinter is large and descending into the inner part of the ear towards the upper part, turn the paper, and extend the splinter to a pair of tweezers, and hold and press on one side and the other; and if the paper is moved by incision, it does not hurt anything; and when the splinter is removed, pour in some oil of strong salt, and heal the wound until the pain is gone.
de la graisse des eulz	of the fat of the eyes
Exinach est une graisse qui est enjanree en toiles des papieres desus, et ce avient plus as enfans c’a nules gens, et grieve mout a lor eulz, et li vienent li catharre as matinees, et ne pueent regardeir la lumiere dou soleil por ceu que les larmes se hastent a lor eulz; et por ceu se couchent il sor lor faices adés, et dorment sus, et sont lor papieres desoz lor sorcilz moistes que li enfleure et li apparance ont covert de l’exinach qui apert en l’oil.	Exinach is a grease that is smeared on the upper part of papers, and it has more in children than in adults, and it hurts their eyes, and they come to have diarrhea in the morning, and they cannot look at the light of the sun because their tears stick to their eyes; and because they lie down, they sleep on their faces adhered, and sleep on top, and their papers are outside their eyelids moist that it swells and appears covered with exinach that opens in oil.

des poilz des papieres	of hairs of papers
Quant em papieres naissent poilz ajostez autre que li naturez, et sont enveillit, si nuisent as eulz, et font venir manieres de maladies si com larmes acostumees et mollifications des papieres et albugine, tant que c’est cause de la destruction des eulz; et est li cure selonc IIII manieres: ou par cautere ensamble feu, ou par medicine ague selonc ceu qu’il est devant ou chapistre de cautere, et est fais ou par incision et costure ou par caines, selonc ceu que je dirai. S’il tarde, si le cope a unes forces, puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez; et quant li plaie iert soudee, et si ert levee li papiere, et ne poindront plus li poil; et c’est li forme des II cainnes que tu feras selonc ceste figure, et selonc ceste quantiteit de lonc et de large:	If it lingers, if the copper has some force, then cure it until it is healed; and when the wound has been soaked, and if it was raised with paper, and they will not grow back again; and this is the form of the two coins that you will make according to this figure, and according to this quantity of length and width:
li ovraiges est telz que tu preignes une aguille subtil, et i boute I fil de soie souef et subtil; puis assemble les chiés et noe l’un et l’autre subtilment, et soit li longesce des filz une palme de lonc; puis ordene en la chasse I autre fil subtil de soie briément, et noe les chief dou fil; puis mette li malaides son chief en ton sain; et soit delez lou soleil si que li ovraiges soit declairiez, car c’est uns ovraiges subtilz et menus, puis boute l’aguille a tout la chasse en la racine dou poil ajosteit, et la fai percier en la papiere hastanment tant que tu la traies desus lou poil natureil; puis estrai le poil jusque sus la chasse, et boute en la chasse celui poil, s’il en i a I ou II ou III ou plusors; puis estrai ta main tant que li poilz veigne fuers a tout la chasse en la papiere avec lou poil natureil.	The work is such that you grasp a fine needle, and bring out the silk thread softly and subtly; then assemble the heads and make them both subtly, and let the length of the threads be one palm long; then order the other fine silk thread briefly, and make the heads of the threads, then put the hairs on your healthy skin; and let it be outside the sun so that the work is hidden, for this is a subtle and small work, then push the needle through the entire length in the root of the raised hair, and pierce it into the paper gently until you pull it out of the natural hair; then pull the hair up to the length of the work, and push that hair into the work, if there is one or two or three or more; then pull your hand so that the hairs come out completely on the entire length with the natural hair.
Et se li chasse est traite et li poilz ne vient fuer avec li, si trairas la chasse au desoz a tout le fil que tu i as ordeneit, tant que li chasse veigne fuer dou pertus desus et que tu la voies par la vision de l’oil; adonques si trairas la chasse et le fil, et clo l’oil et lou laisse clo II jors ou III, tant que li poil s’aerde en son leu et naisse li char sus; et se li poilz est petis, si acompaigne I poil lonc des chevoulz naturez, et soit alevez avec celui ou tu le laisse, tant qu’il soit eslongiez et puis le lieve.	And if the arrow is treated and the hairs do not grow back with it, you should re-treat the arrow using the same thread that you had previously ordered, until the arrow becomes fully dry and you can see it through oil; then you should remove the arrow and the thread, close the wound and leave it open for two or three days, until the hair grows back in its place and on the skin; if the hairs are small, accompany them with one long hair from the tail of a wild beast, and elevate it with the other that you leave, until it is fully extended and then remove it.
de la porriture de l’oil	of the preparation of the oil
Quant ceste maladie qui est apelee «aleacrati» ou li porriture vient en l’oil, si en i a de II manieres: l’une natureil, et l’autre innatureil.	When this disease, which is called "aleacrati" or the putrefaction, comes from the oil, there are two ways: one natural and the other unnatural.
Et avient par soudement de plaie, ou de tailleure ou de cautere, et par semblans choses.	And it occurs from the wound, or from the cutting or cauterizing, and from similar things.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige en li est que tu fendes celle soudure, et dessevre les levres de li, et met dedens tentes de lin, et la lie tant qu’elle soit sanee; et ne covient mie que tu uses en la cure de li de choses que sechent et restraignent.	And the way of the work in it is that you break that suture, and dry the lips of it, and put inside linen tents, and bandage it until it is healed; and it is only necessary to use in its care things that dry and restrict.
Car se tu fais ceu, si revient li maladie pire que li premiere; mais i oevre de choses amollissans, si com fenugreic; et l’arose d’aigue ou altee et semence de lin soient cuites, et oignemens dyaquilon fondut en aucun des oiles, et i envoloupe une tente, et le cure de ceu.	For if you do this, the disease becomes worse than the first; but in the work of things that are softening, such as fenugreek; and the rose of vinegar or alcohol and seeds of linseed boiled, and ointments of quicksilver melted into any of the oils, and there is wrapped a tent, and the care of this.
Et li tresors de ta cure si est que tu te dones en garde qu’ele ne soude mie selonc la forme qu’elle fut devant; et cist ovraiges que nos avons dit nen est fuers que adresemens de ceste maladie, qu’elle ne reviegne selonc la forme qu’elle fut devant.	And the treasures of your care are that you take precautions so that it does not return to its former form; and this work that we have said is only an approach to this disease, that it does not return to its former form.
de la char qui vient en l’oil	of the oil that comes in the jar
Ceste maladie que est desoz qui vraiement est apelee «axacrati», et est naturelz et accidens.	This disease that is truly called "axacrati", and is natural and accidental.
Li accidens vient de plaie et de fendure et de cautere et de choses semblans; et li voie de l’ovraige en li si est que tu preignes un aguille, en coi il ait I fil double, et la fiche en la char, et li fai percier des le senestre larmier tant c’a destre, si que li filz veigne en II chiés de la char; puis estent la char au desus a tout l’aguille, et la cope a I spatumile large.	The accident comes from wounds and cuts and cauterization and similar things; and the way of the work is that you hold an needle, in which it has the thread double, and the skein in the jar, and make it pierce from the right arm to the left, so that the thread comes out of both arms; then place the jar above the whole needle, and the cloth wide.
